$(document).ready(function() { var $subscribe = $('#tns-subscribe'); var $modal = $subscribe.find('.modal'); var $header = $modal.find('.header'); var $close = $modal.find('.close'); var $content = $modal.find('.content'); var $footer = $modal.find('.footer'); var $subscribe\_button = $modal.find('.subscribe-button'); /// Init Swiper var $subscribe\_swiper = new Swiper('.tns-subscribe-swiper', { allowTouchMove: false, loop: false, slidesPerView: 1, autoplay: false, spaceBetween: 0, navigation : false, observer : true, preventInteractionOnTransition: true, a11y: false, noSwipingSelector: 'button' }); /// Init window.tns.subscribe window.tns = window.tns || {} window.tns.subscribe = { prepop : false, section : '', context : '', screen : 0, open : function() { /// Reset the modal window.tns.subscribe.screen = 0; if (window.tns.subscribe.prepop === true) { $subscribe\_button.click(); } }, close : function() { window.tns.subscribe.screen = 0; $subscribe.stop().css({ opacity : 0, display : 'block' }); $modal.stop().transition({ duration : 333, opacity : 0, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $subscribe.stop().transition({ duration : 333, opacity : 0, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }, function() { $subscribe.stop().css({ opacity : 0, display : 'none' }); $('body').css({ overflowY : 'auto' }); $('.tns-subscribe-swiper-button-next').text('NEXT'); $modal.stop().transition({ maxHeight : 370, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $content.stop().transition({ bottom : 0, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $footer.stop().transition({ bottom : -60, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); }); }, submit : async function(direction) { /// Track the step completed var action\_taken = ''; /// Init the payload object var payload = { recaptcha\_token : '', section : window.tns.subscribe.section, screen : null, data : { EMAIL : '', FNAME : '', LNAME : '', COMPANY : '', COUNTRY : '', ZIPCODE : '', JOBLEVEL : '', JOBROLE : '', ORGEMP : '', ORGDESC : '', ORGINDUS : '', LINKPROURL : '' }, errors : \[\] }; /// Determine the target\_screen var screen = window.tns.subscribe.screen; payload.screen = window.tns.subscribe.screen; console.log('\[TNS Subscribe\]', payload); var target\_screen = window.tns.subscribe.screen; if (direction === 'prev') { target\_screen = screen - 1; } if (direction === 'next') { target\_screen = screen + 1; } /// Gather the values from the form $('.subscribe-input').each(function() { var key = $(this).data('key'); var value = $(this).val(); payload.data\[key\] = value; }); /// Validate the values for the current screen if (screen === 0) { action\_taken = 'newsletter\_subscribe'; if (!payload.data.EMAIL || !validator.isEmail(payload.data.EMAIL)) { payload.errors.push({ key : 'EMAIL', msg : 'EMAIL is required.' }); } } if (screen === 1) { action\_taken = 'demo\_data\_1'; var required = \[ 'FNAME', 'LNAME', 'COMPANY', 'COUNTRY' \] required.map((key) => { if (!payload.data\[key\]) { payload.errors.push({ key : key, msg : key + ' is required.' }) } }); if (payload.data.COUNTRY === 'US' && !payload.data.ZIPCODE) { payload.errors.push({ key : 'ZIPCODE', msg : 'ZIPCODE is required.' }) } } if (screen === 2) { action\_taken = 'demo\_data\_2'; var required = \[ 'JOBLEVEL', 'JOBROLE', 'ORGEMP', 'ORGDESC', 'ORGINDUS', // 'LINKPROURL' \] if (payload.data.ORGEMP === 'not-working') { /// Remove ORGDESC and ORGINDUS from the required array required = required.filter(function(item) { return item !== 'ORGDESC' && item !== 'ORGINDUS' }) } required.map((key) => { if (!payload.data\[key\]) { payload.errors.push({ key : key, msg : key + ' is required.' }) } }); if (payload.data.JOBLEVEL === 'other') { var other\_value = $('.subscribe-job-level-other').val(); if (!other\_value) { payload.errors.push({ key : 'JOBLEVEL', msg : 'JOBLEVEL is required.' }) } else { payload.data.JOBLEVEL = other\_value; } } if (payload.data.JOBROLE === 'other') { var other\_value = $('.subscribe-job-role-other').val(); if (!other\_value) { payload.errors.push({ key : 'JOBROLE', msg : 'JOBROLE is required.' }) } else { payload.data.JOBROLE = other\_value; } } if (payload.data.ORGDESC === 'other') { var other\_value = $('.subscribe-organization-description-other').val(); if (!other\_value) { payload.errors.push({ key : 'ORGDESC', msg : 'ORGDESC is required.' }) } else { payload.data.ORGDESC = other\_value; } } if (payload.data.ORGINDUS === 'other') { var other\_value = $('.subscribe-industry-other').val(); if (!other\_value) { payload.errors.push({ key : 'ORGINDUS', msg : 'ORGINDUS is required.' }) } else { payload.data.ORGINDUS = other\_value; } } // if (!payload.data.LINKPROURL.includes('linkedin.com')) { // payload.errors.push({ // key : 'LINKPROURL', // msg : 'LINKPROURL must be a linkedin.com url.' // }) // } } if (direction === 'next' && payload.errors.length) { var $error\_input = $('.subscribe-input\[data-key="' + payload.errors\[0\].key + '"'); $error\_input.addClass('error').focus(); $error\_input.parent().find('.form-field-info').addClass('error'); console.log('ERROR', payload); if (direction === 'next') { return payload; } } /// /// POST /no-cache/subscribe/ /// if (direction === 'next') { payload.recaptcha\_token = window.tns.turnstile.token; var result = await $.post('/no-cache/subscribe/', payload); result = JSON.parse(result); console.log('\[TNS SUBSCRIBE\]', result); if (result.errors.length) { console.log('\[TNS SUBSCRIBE\]', result.errors\[0\].msg); if (result.errors\[0\].msg == 'UNSUBSCRIBED') { window.tns.subscribe.resubscribe(); } if (result.errors\[0\].msg == 'TURNSTILE\_FAILED') { window.tns.subscribe.resubscribe(); } return payload; } /// Re-enabled the subscribe button $('.subscribe-button').html('SUBSCRIBE') $('.subscribe-button').attr('disabled', false) window.dataLayer.push({ 'event' : 'subscribe', 'context' : window.tns.subscribe.context, 'action\_taken' : action\_taken }); } /// Toggle the footer UI if (target\_screen === 0) { $('.tns-subscribe-swiper-button-next').text('NEXT'); $modal.stop().transition({ maxHeight : 370, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $content.stop().transition({ bottom : 0, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $footer.stop().transition({ bottom : -60, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); } if (target\_screen === 1) { $('.tns-subscribe-swiper-button-next').text('NEXT'); $modal.stop().transition({ maxHeight : 600, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $content.stop().transition({ bottom : 60, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $footer.stop().transition({ bottom : 0, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); setTimeout(function() { $('.subscribe-firstname').focus(); }, 400); } if (target\_screen === 2) { $('.tns-subscribe-swiper-button-next').text('SUBMIT'); setTimeout(function() { $('.subscribe-job-level').focus(); }, 400); } if (target\_screen === 3) { $modal.stop().transition({ maxHeight : 710, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $content.stop().transition({ bottom : 0, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $footer.stop().transition({ bottom : -60, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); } /// Transition to the prev or next slide $subscribe\_swiper.slideTo(target\_screen, 333, true); window.tns.subscribe.screen = target\_screen; $('.subscribe-current-slide').text(window.tns.subscribe.screen); $subscribe\_button.attr('disabled', false); }, resubscribe: function() { /// If a reader has previously unsubscribed they /// must use the Mailchimp hosted form to resubscribe /// Reset the UI to screen 0 window.tns.subscribe.screen = 0; $subscribe\_swiper.slideTo(0, 333, true); $('.tns-subscribe-swiper-button-next').text('NEXT'); $modal.stop().transition({ maxHeight : 370, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $content.stop().transition({ bottom : 0, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $footer.stop().transition({ bottom : -60, duration : 333, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); /// Hide the subscribe form and reset the button $('.copy-screen-0').hide(); $('.form-field-email').hide(); $('.subscribe-button').html('SUBSCRIBE') $('.subscribe-button').attr('disabled', false) /// Show the re-subscribe form $('.form-field-resubscribe').show(); $('.resubscribe-button').off('click'); $('.resubscribe-button').on('click', function($event) { window.open('http://eepurl.com/bMg5kH', '\_blank'); // DO NOT transition to the next slide // because they'll still be in "pending" mode // so we can't collect any data. // $modal.stop().transition({ // maxHeight : 600, // duration : 333, // easing : 'easeOutQuad' // }); // }, 400); // $subscribe\_swiper.slideTo(1, 333, true); // window.tns.subscribe.screen = 1; }); } } /// Remove all error classes on keyup $('.subscribe-input').on('keyup', function($event) { if ($event.key === 'Enter') return; $('.subscribe-input').removeClass('error'); $('.form-field-info').removeClass('error'); }); $('select.subscribe-input').on('change', function($event) { $('.subscribe-input').removeClass('error'); $('.form-field-info').removeClass('error'); } }); /// Handle other input toggle $('.subscribe-has-other').on('change', function($event) { var value = $(this).val(); var $other\_input = $(this).next(); var $other\_clear = $(this).next().next(); $(document).ready(function() { /// Handle TNS Daily subscription var $poll = $('.tns-poll\[data-instanceID="6812736a1df97"\]'); var $tnsNewsletterEmailInput = $poll.find('.tns-poll-postroll-daily-input'); var $tnsNewsletterSubmitButton = $poll.find('.tns-poll-postroll-daily-button'); $tnsNewsletterEmailInput.on('keyup', function($event) { $(this).removeClass('error'); if ($event.which === 13) { $tnsNewsletterSubmitButton.click(); } }); $tnsNewsletterSubmitButton.on('click', function() { var email = $tnsNewsletterEmailInput.val(); window.tns.subscribe.prepop = true; window.tns.subscribe.context = 'tns\_voxpop\_postroll'; $('#tns-subscribe').find('.subscribe-email').val(email); $('#tns-subscribe').find('.subscribe-button').click(); window.tns.subscribe.open(); }); });

$(document).ready(function() { var $poll = $('.tns-poll\[data-instanceID="6812736a1df97"\]'); var $option = $poll.find('.option'); var sponsor\_slug = ''; var voxpop = 'true'; /// string 'true' || 'false' var voted = localStorage.getItem('tns\_poll\_vote\_22754645'); if (voted) voted = JSON.parse(voted); /// /// Handle vote /// $option.on('click', function($event) { var $thisOption = $(this); var poll\_ID = '22754645'; var instance\_ID = '6812736a1df97'; var question\_ID = null; var answer\_ID = null; var captchaToken = null; var pollData = null; if ($poll.hasClass('done')) return; async.series(\[ setStatusClasses, obtainCaptchaToken, revealPercentages, submitVote, displayResults, handlePostroll \], function(result) { if (result) console.log(result); }); function setStatusClasses(next) { $poll.addClass('done'); $option.removeClass('active'); $thisOption.addClass('active'); $thisOption.addClass('selected'); question\_ID = $thisOption.data('questionid'); answer\_ID = $thisOption.data('answerid'); return next(); } function obtainCaptchaToken(next) { captchaToken = window.tns.turnstile.token; return next(); } function revealPercentages(next) { var delay = 21; var i = 0; $poll.find('.option-percentage').each(function() { $(this).transition({ delay : delay \* i, duration : 99, opacity : 1, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); i++; }); return next(); } function submitVote(next) { var payload = { poll\_ID : '22754645', instance\_ID : instance\_ID, question\_ID : question\_ID, answer\_ID : answer\_ID, recaptcha\_token : captchaToken, sponsor : sponsor\_slug } console.log('\[tns-poll\] Sending poll vote ...') $.ajax({ url : '/no-cache/polls-vote/', type : 'post', data : payload, statusCode : { 429 : function() { $poll.removeClass('done'); $option.removeClass('active'); $poll.find('.option-percentage').css({ opacity : 0 }); var poll\_type = 'inline'; if (voxpop === 'true') poll\_type = 'voxpop'; var event\_payload = { event : 'poll', poll\_action : 'rate-limited', poll\_type : poll\_type, poll\_id : '22754645', question\_ID : question\_ID, answer\_ID : answer\_ID } if (sponsor\_slug) { event\_payload.sponsor = sponsor\_slug; } window.dataLayer.push(event\_payload) var msg = '429  Whoa, facile tigr.'; msg += 'You\\'re being rate-limited.'; msg += 'If you\\'re human, take it easy and try again in an hour.'; console.log(msg); } } }).done(function(data, statusText, xhr) { if (data) data = JSON.parse(data); pollData = data; console.log('\[tns-poll\] Result from vote endpoint:'); console.log(data); /// Pre-construct the event\_payload var poll\_type = 'inline'; if (voxpop === 'true') poll\_type = 'voxpop'; var event\_payload = { event : 'poll', poll\_action : null, poll\_type : poll\_type, poll\_id : '22754645', question\_ID : question\_ID, answer\_ID : answer\_ID } if (sponsor\_slug) { event\_payload.sponsor = sponsor\_slug; } if (data.bot === true) { event\_payload.poll\_action = 'recaptcha-fail'; console.log('\[tns-poll\] Suspected bot vote due to recaptcha fail.'); window.dataLayer.push(event\_payload); event\_payload.instance\_ID = instance\_ID; console.log(event\_payload); return next(); } if (!voted && data.unique\_vote === true) { event\_payload.poll\_action = 'vote'; console.log('\[tns-poll\] Unique vote detected, firing GA4 event.'); window.dataLayer.push(event\_payload); event\_payload.instance\_ID = instance\_ID; console.log(event\_payload); delete payload.recaptcha\_token; localStorage.setItem('tns\_poll\_vote\_22754645', JSON.stringify(payload)); console.log('\[tns-poll\] Set localStorage item.'); } else { event\_payload.poll\_action = 'duplicate-vote-attempt'; console.log('\[tns-poll\] Detected duplicate vote, did not fire GA4 event.'); event\_payload.instance\_ID = instance\_ID; console.log(event\_payload); delete payload.recaptcha\_token; localStorage.setItem('tns\_poll\_vote\_22754645', JSON.stringify(payload)); } return next(); }); } function displayResults(next) { var highestPercentage = 0; var totalVotes = parseInt(pollData.totalVotes); var totalPercentage = 0; $option.each(function() { var optionAnswerID = $(this).data('answerid'); var percentage = 0; pollData.results.map(result => { if (result.answer\_ID === optionAnswerID) { percentage = parseInt(result.percentage); totalPercentage += percentage; if (percentage > highestPercentage) { highestPercentage = percentage; $option.removeClass('active'); $(this).addClass('active'); } } }); var $resultsBar = $(this).find('.option-results'); var $percentDisplay = $(this).find('.option-percentage'); var digit = 0; var uptickPercentDisplay = setInterval(function() { if (digit >= percentage) { clearInterval(uptickPercentDisplay); return; } digit++; $percentDisplay.html(digit + '%'); }, 3); if (percentage === 0) { $percentDisplay.html('0%'); } $resultsBar.transition({ width : percentage + '%', duration : 777, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }) }); return next(); } function handlePostroll(next) { if (voxpop !== 'true') { console.log('\[tns-poll\] Inline poll detected, skipping post-roll ...'); return next(); } console.log('\[tns-poll\] Voxpop poll detected, firing post-roll ...'); var targetHeight = $poll.find('.post-roll-block').outerHeight(true); $poll.find('.post-roll').transition({ delay : 555, height : targetHeight, duration : 777, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); setTimeout(function() { $poll.find('.post-roll').addClass('open'); if (window.tns.voxpop && window.tns.voxpop.vote) { window.tns.voxpop.vote(pollData, 777); } }, 777); } }); /// /// Handle firing the impression event, but only when /// the poll enters the viewport. /// function isInViewport($element) { var elementTop = $element.offset().top; var elementBottom = elementTop + $element.outerHeight(); var viewportTop = $(window).scrollTop(); var viewportBottom = viewportTop + $(window).height(); return elementBottom > viewportTop && elementTop = windowHeight) { targetHeight = windowHeight - 40; } $voxpopModal.stop().transition({ height : targetHeight, duration : delay || 333, easing : 'snap' }); }, open : function(params) { $('body').css({ overflow : 'hidden' }); $voxpopScreen.stop().css({ opacity : 0, display : 'block' }); $voxpopScreen.stop().transition({ duration : 333, opacity : 1, easing : 'snap' }); $voxpopModal.stop().css({ opacity : 0, display : 'block' }); window.tns.voxpop.resize(); $voxpopModal.stop().transition({ delay : 333, duration : 121, opacity : 1, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); /// /// Record an impression event /// if (!voted) { var event\_payload = { poll\_action : 'impression', poll\_type : 'voxpop', poll\_id : '22754645' } if (sponsor\_slug) { event\_payload.sponsor = sponsor\_slug; } console.log('\[Voxpop\] Impression detected, firing GA4 event.'); event\_payload.event = 'poll'; window.dataLayer.push(event\_payload); event\_payload.instance\_ID = instance\_ID; console.log(event\_payload); } }, vote : function(pollData, delay) { console.log('\[Voxpop\] Firing post-vote resize.'); setTimeout(function() { window.tns.voxpop.resize(delay); }, 555); }, close : function() { $voxpopScreen.stop().css({ opacity : 0, display : 'block' }); $voxpopModal.stop().transition({ duration : 333, opacity : 0, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }); $voxpopScreen.stop().transition({ duration : 333, opacity : 0, easing : 'easeOutQuad' }, function() { $voxpopScreen.stop().css({ opacity : 0, display : 'none' }); $('body').css({ overflowY : 'auto' }); }); } } $('.tns-voxpop-close').on('click', function() { window.tns.voxpop.close(); }); $('.tns-voxpop-screen').on('click', function() { window.tns.voxpop.close(); }); $(window).on('resize', function() { window.tns.voxpop.resize(); }); /// /// Auto-open Voxpop based on the \`open-voxpop\` query param? /// var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search); if (urlParams.get('open-voxpop')) { window.tns.voxpop.open(); } });

$(document).ready(function() { function toggleMobileNav() { if ($('.masthead-menu-icon').hasClass('active')) { $('.masthead-menu-icon').removeClass('active'); $('#tns-header-masthead').removeClass('dark'); $('.masthead-menu-close-icon').stop().transition({ opacity : 0, duration : 0, easeing : 'snap' }, function() { $(this).css({ display : 'none' }); }); $('.masthead-menu-icon').stop().css({ display : 'block' }).transition({ opacity : 1, duration : 333, easeing : 'snap' }); $('.masthead-search-icon').stop().css({ display : 'block' }).transition({ opacity : 1, duration : 121, easeing : 'snap' }); var height = '60px'; var paddingBottom = '0px'; $('body').css({ overflowX : 'hidden', overflowY : 'auto' }); } else { $('.masthead-menu-icon').addClass('active'); $('#tns-header-masthead').addClass('dark'); $('.masthead-menu-icon').stop().transition({ opacity : 0, duration : 0, easeing : 'snap' }, function() { $(this).css({ display : 'none' }); }); $('.masthead-search-icon').stop().transition({ opacity : 0, duration : 333, easeing : 'snap' }, function() { $(this).css({ display : 'none' }); }); $('.masthead-menu-close-icon').stop().css({ display : 'block' }).transition({ opacity : 1, duration : 333, easeing : 'snap' }); var height = window.screen.height; var paddingBottom = '200px'; $('body').css({ overflowX : 'hidden', overflowY : 'hidden' }); } $('.mobile-nav-dropdown').scrollTop(0); $('.mobile-nav-dropdown').stop().transition({ height : height, paddingBottom : paddingBottom, duration : 222, easeing : 'snap' }); } $('.masthead-menu-icon').on('click', function($event) { $event.preventDefault(); window.dataLayer.push({ 'event' : 'nav\_click', 'target' : 'mobile\_nav' }); toggleMobileNav(); }); $('.masthead-menu-close-icon').on('click', function($event) { $event.preventDefault(); toggleMobileNav(); }); });

$(document).ready(function() { function toggleSearch() { if ($('.masthead-search-icon').hasClass('active')) { $('.masthead-search-icon').removeClass('active'); $('#tns-header-masthead').removeClass('dark'); $('.masthead-search-close-icon').stop().transition({ opacity : 0, duration : 0, easeing : 'snap' }, function() { $(this).css({ display : 'none' }); }); $('.masthead-search-icon').stop().css({ display : 'block' }).transition({ opacity : 1, duration : 121, easeing : 'snap' }); $('.masthead-menu-icon').stop().css({ display : 'block' }).transition({ opacity : 1, duration : 121, easeing : 'snap' }); var height = '60px'; $('body').css({ overflowX : 'hidden', overflowY : 'auto' }); $('#tns-header-search-form').removeClass('active-search'); $('body').removeClass('search-hidden'); } else { $('.masthead-search-icon').addClass('active'); $('#tns-header-masthead').addClass('dark'); $('.masthead-menu-icon').stop().transition({ opacity : 0, duration : 333, easeing : 'snap' }, function() { $(this).css({ display : 'none' }); }); $('.masthead-search-icon').stop().transition({ opacity : 0, duration : 0, easeing : 'snap' }, function() { $(this).css({ display : 'none' }); }); $('.masthead-search-close-icon').stop().css({ display : 'block' }).transition({ opacity : 1, duration : 121, easeing : 'snap' }); $('#tns-header-search-form').addClass('active-search'); $('body').addClass('search-hidden'); var height = window.screen.height; $('body').css({ overflowX : 'hidden', overflowY : 'hidden' }); } $('.search-dropdown').stop().transition({ height : height, duration : 222, easeing : 'snap' }); setTimeout(function() { $('.search-input').focus(); }, 555); } $('.masthead-search-icon').on('click', function($event) { $event.preventDefault(); window.dataLayer.push({ 'event' : 'nav\_click', 'target' : 'search', }); $('.search-input').blur(); toggleSearch(); }); $('.masthead-search-close-icon').on('click', function() { toggleSearch(); }); });

Search

   \*\*\*thumbnail\*\*\*    \*\*\*title\*\*\*    \*\*\*byline\*\*\* &mdash;   \*\*\*excerpt\*\*\*      function truncateString(str, length) { return str.length > length ? str.substring(0, length - 3) + '...' : str } function stripTags(html) { var tmp = document.createElement("DIV"); tmp.innerHTML = html; return tmp.textContent || tmp.innerText; } $(document).ready(function() { window.search = window.search || {} window.search.start = 1 window.search.attributionToken = '' window.search.nextPageToken = '' search.results = function(query) { if (!query) return; if (window.search.start == 1) { $('.search-results-list').empty(); } search.url = '/no-cache/search-results?' search.url += 'q=' + query if (window.search.attributionToken != '') { search.url += '&attribution\_token=' + window.search.attributionToken search.url += '&next\_page\_token=' + window.search.nextPageToken } /// GA Event to track searches/queries window.dataLayer.push({ 'event' : 'search', 'query' : query }); console.log(search.url) $.get(search.url, function(response) { response = JSON.parse(response) console.log('Search Query Response:') console.log(response) window.search.attributionToken = response.attributionToken window.search.nextPageToken = response.nextPageToken console.log('Next Page Token:') console.log(window.search.nextPageToken) var results = response.results if (results.length == 0) { $('.search-results-list').html('Your search returned no results. Please try again.'); $('.search-results-more-button').hide(); return } $.each(results, function(index, item) { var data = item.document.derivedStructData var title = data.title.replace(' - The New Stack', '') var link = data.link.replace('https://thenewstack.io', '') var authors = item.document.structData\['x-tns-authors'\] var excerpt = data.snippets\[0\].snippet // var datePublishedMicroseconds = data.datePublished // var datePublished = new Date(datePublishedMicroseconds / 1000) var dateModifiedMicroseconds = data.dateModified var dateModified = new Date(dateModifiedMicroseconds / 1000) var day = dateModified.getDate() var month = dateModified.toLocaleString('default', { month: 'short' }) var year = dateModified.getFullYear() var suffix = '' if (\[1, 21, 31\].includes(day)) { suffix = 'st' } else if (\[2, 22\].includes(day)) { suffix = 'nd' } else if (\[3, 23\].includes(day)) { suffix = 'rd' } else { suffix = 'th' } var dateline = day + suffix + ' ' + month + ' ' + year /// Handle Author Page results differently var isAuthorPage = link.includes('/author/'); var result = $('#search-results-item').html() result = result.split('\*\*\*itemNum\*\*\*').join(index) result = result.split('\*\*\*permalink\*\*\*').join(link) result = result.split('\*\*\*title\*\*\*').join(title) // var postDate = moment(meta\['x-tns-post-date'\]); // var formattedDate = postDate.format('Do MMM YYYY'); var byline = '' if (!isAuthorPage) { byline = dateline + ', by ' + stripTags(authors) result = result.split('\*\*\*byline\*\*\*').join(byline) } else { byline = dateline result = result.split('\*\*\*byline\*\*\*').join(byline) } result = result.split('\*\*\*excerpt\*\*\*').join(excerpt) $('.search-results-list').append(result); // if (isAuthorPage) { // $itemElement = $('.search-results-item-' + index); // $itemElement.find('.search-results-item-byline').hide(); // } }); $('.search-results-list').show(); $('.search-results-more-button').show(); }); return; } /// Form bindings $('.search-input').on('keyup', function($event) { if ($event.key !== 'Enter') return var query = $('.search-input').val() window.search.start = 1 window.search.attributionToken = '' window.search.nextPageToken = '' window.search.results(query) }); $('.search-submit').on('click', function($event) { var query = $('.search-input').val(); window.search.start = 1 window.search.attributionToken = '' window.search.nextPageToken = '' window.search.results(query); }); });

### What Are the Main Goals of Data Visualization?

Its important to set goals and objectives when creating data visualizations. Here are a few to consider when putting together your own data visualizations:

*   Data visualizations are useful for highlighting trends, patterns and correlations in data.
*   Data visualization is an effective decision-making tool that enables key individuals to make well-informed decisions backed by data.
*   Data visualizations make it easier to make sense of large datasets and combine different datasets from various sources.
*   Its an effective way of using storytelling to communicate data-backed ideas.
*   Data visualizations need to hold the target audiences attention while being easy to understand and interpret.
*   Data visualizations make it easier to monitor important metrics and keep an eye on key performance indicators (KPIs).

## Best Practices for Data Visualization

Here are a few best practices to keep in mind when creating visualizations.

### 1\. Have a Goal in Mind

When creating data visualizations, first understand the type of data youre working with and have an idea of the type of insights youd like to derive from them. Keep in mind the information you want to communicate, its importance and the audience you are presenting to.

### 2\. Choose the Right Visualization Tool

After setting goals for your visualization, consider the right tools to help you present your data. There are code libraries and no-code/low-code platforms, depending on the use case, and they each have their own strengths.

**No-Code/Low-Code Platforms**

With little to no knowledge of how to code, you can create engaging data visualizations that capture the message youre trying to communicate. Here are a few popular visualization platforms that can enable you to create visualizations, dashboards and reports:

*   **Tableau:** Tableau is a visual analytics platform that enables users to create interactive charts, maps and dashboards. The effortless drag-and-drop functionality of the platform enables users to quickly create interactive visualizations with a wide range of charts, graph and interactive elements, while also enabling users to integrate programming languages such as Python and R.

![](https://cdn.thenewstack.io/media/2023/01/31bb2e23-image3.png)

Tableau

*   **Power BI:** Power BI is a popular business intelligence platform that allows professionals to create interactive dashboards, charts and graphs, offering a wide range of options and interactive elements while being user-friendly and intuitive.

![](https://cdn.thenewstack.io/media/2023/01/d070f9a8-image2.png)

\[Power BI

*   **Looker Studio (formerly Google Data Studio):** Looker Studio is a platform that allows users to create customizable dashboards and reports. It provides users with an effective option to create professional-quality visualizations for free and without the need to write code.

![](https://cdn.thenewstack.io/media/2023/01/095bca66-image8.png)

Looker Studio

**Data Visualization Libraries**

On the other hand, depending on the use case, you can use code to create data visualizations. For visualizations, you can build and use packages created in JavaScript, Python and R.

**Python**

Python is a versatile programming language used extensively for data science and machine learning. Several data visualization libraries are in Python, and you can select libraries depending on your projects needs.

Here are a few of the most widely used libraries in Python:

*   [Matplotlib](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/matplotlib-tutorial-visualize-time-series-data-matplotlib-influxdb/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns)
*   [Seaborn](https://seaborn.pydata.org/)
*   [Bokeh](https://docs.bokeh.org/en/latest/)
*   [Plotly](https://github.com/plotly/plotly.py)
*   [Streamlit](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/visualize-data-streamlit-influxdb/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns)

**JavaScript**

JavaScript is a popular programming language used to build web applications and interactive elements on websites and create data visualizations. A few popular libraries for creating visualizations are as follows:

*   [D3.js](https://d3js.org/)
*   [Chart.js](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/visualizing-time-series-data-chartjs-influxdb/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns)
*   [Highcharts](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/visualizing-time-series-data-with-highcharts-library-influxdb/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns)
*   [Plotly.js](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/data-visualizations-with-influxdb-integrating-plotly-js/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns)
*   [Leaflet](https://leafletjs.com/examples.html)
*   [Echarts](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/visualizing-time-series-data-echarts-influxdb/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns)
*   [Recharts](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/recharts-influxdb-tutorial-visualize-iot-sensor-data-reactjs/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns)
*   [Victory Native](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/data-visualizations-react-native-victory-charts-tutorial/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns)
*   [Nivo](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/data-visualization-reactjs-nivo-influxdb/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns)

**R**

R is a programming language and software environment used for statistical computing and visualizations. With R, youll have access to several libraries and packages for creating a wide range of visualizations, including simple plots and interactive graphics.

Here are a few widely used R packages for data visualizations:

*   [ggplot2](https://ggplot2.tidyverse.org/)
*   [Highcharter](https://jkunst.com/highcharter/)
*   [Plotly](https://github.com/plotly/plotly.R)

### 3\. Choose the Right Type of Visualization

Picking the right type of visualization can greatly improve clarity and readability, and ensure your visualizations are engaging. When using these visualizations, ensure that you make wise comparisons and use charts well-suited for the data type. The right visualization depends on your goals, data type and audience.

Here are some charts and what theyre most useful for:

*   **Bar charts:** Bar charts are graphs with rectangular bars used for creating visuals for categorical data. They are useful for showing distributions and are commonly used as theyre a quick way of communicating information and comparing values.
*   **Line graphs:** Line graphs use lines to connect different data points. Theyre helpful when creating a graph that presents trends and patterns in data, such as [time series data](https://www.influxdata.com/what-is-time-series-data/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns). Some [examples](https://www.influxdata.com/how-to-visualize-time-series-data/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns) are changes in weather, stock prices, sales, etc.
*   **Scatter plots:** Scatter plots show relationships between variables and are helpful when representing how variables influence each other or identifying data patterns.
*   **Pie charts:** Pie charts are simple, effective charts that use a circular diagram, with each portion of the pie representing the relative size of the data. Theyre used to show how a quantity or percentage is distributed, or has changed over time, by using multiple charts to represent different time periods.
*   **Box plots (or box and whisker plots):** Box plots are graphs used to present the minimum, maximum, median, first quartile and third quartile of a dataset. Theyre especially useful for seeing the overall shape of your dataset and pointing out outliers.
*   **Violin plots:** Violin plots are similar to box plots and are used to visualize the distribution of a dataset. They can be used to show a datasets minimum, maximum, median, and quartiles and the distribution of the data using kernel density plots. You can use them to compare data distribution between different groups or to identify outliers in data.
*   **Heatmaps:** Heatmaps are colored matrices used to present data values; darker colors are used to represent high values, while cooler colors represent lower values. Heatmaps are useful for identifying noteworthy variations in data as well as pointing out patterns and trends.

**Examples**

Lets create a few data visualization examples with code using popular Python libraries:

*   *   **Bar charts:** Here, well create a bar chart using the values in **x** for the _data values_ axis and the values in **y** for the _frequency_ axis. Create a bar chart with Matplotlib using the **bar()** function.

import matplotlib.pyplot as plt # Data to plot x = \[1, 2, 3, 4\] y = \[10, 20, 30, 40\] # Create the bar chart plt.bar(x, y, width=0.5, color='b') # Add labels and title plt.xlabel('Data values') plt.ylabel('Frequency') plt.title('Data distribution') # Show the plot plt.show()

    import seaborn as sns import numpy as np # Generate data x = np.random.randint(1, 10, size=30) y = np.random.randint(1, 30, size=30) # Create the violin plot sns.violinplot(x, y) # Add labels and title plt.xlabel('Data values') plt.ylabel('Frequency') plt.title('Data distribution') # Show the plot plt.show()

    import seaborn as sns
    
    import numpy as np
    
    \# Generate data
    
    x \= np.random.randint(1, 10, size\=30)
    
    y \= np.random.randint(1, 30, size\=30)
    
    \# Create the violin plot
    
    sns.violinplot(x, y)
    
    \# Add labels and title
    
    plt.xlabel('Data values')
    
    plt.ylabel('Frequency')
    
    plt.title('Data distribution')

    from bokeh.plotting import figure, show from bokeh.io import output\_notebook import numpy as np # Generate data x = np.arange(20) y = np.random.randint(1, 20, size=20) # Create the line graph p = figure(title="Line graph", x\_axis\_label="x", y\_axis\_label="y") p.line(x, y) # Show the plot output\_notebook() show(p)

    from bokeh.plotting import figure, show
    
    from bokeh.io import output\_notebook
    
    import numpy as np
    
    \# Generate data
    
    x \= np.arange(20)
    
    y \= np.random.randint(1, 20, size\=20)
    
    \# Create the line graph
    
    p \= figure(title\="Line graph", x\_axis\_label\="x", y\_axis\_label\="y")
    
    p.line(x, y)
    
    \# Show the plot
    
    output\_notebook()
    
    show(p)

You can learn more about data visualization tools [here](https://www.datacamp.com/blog/12-of-the-best-data-visualizations-tools).

### 4\. Use Succinct Labels and Titles

Its important to use labels and titles for your visualizations and ensure theyre easy to understand. These labels should provide context and inform the reader what the graph is trying to communicate.

Other important practices to keep in mind for titles and labels are using fonts that are easy to read, making sure the fonts are large enough, minding the positioning of your labels and using colors that are also easy to read.

You should also avoid having too many labels close together, which creates clutter and affects the readability of the text, and avoid unnecessary abbreviations; if you need to use abbreviations, include what they mean in a key within the report.

### 5\. Choose the Right Colors

Colors play an important role in data visualizations as they help keep your audience engaged with the content of your dashboard, or report and draw the audiences attention to important information youre trying to point out.

When picking a color scheme, you can choose to stay on brand (for example, using your companys brand colors) while keeping in mind the readability of your titles, labels, charts, etc. Try not to use too many colors, and ensure your visualizations are appealing. At the same time, you should consider the [psychology of color](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Color_psychology) as it influences your audiences reaction. Finally, consider people with visual impairments when picking color schemes for your visualization.

In essence, stick to a clear and consistent color scheme for your visualizations.

### 6\. Avoid Clutter and Unnecessary Visual Elements

A good data visualization is easy to understand, engaging and uncluttered. Having too many things going on at once in your visualization can distract your audience from the insights theyre supposed to take away from your work.

To improve the readability of your visualization, use simple designs and avoid unnecessary elements. Unnecessary elements could be too many labels, distracting background images and patterns, unnecessary data points or gridlines that arent relevant. Ensure your titles and labels are easy to read and comprehend and make sure theres adequate spacing between charts and other components. Keep your designs simple and focused on the insights youre trying to get across.

> Youll need to clean and preprocess your data to ensure its free from errors and anomalies.

### 7\. Use Data That Is Clean and Up to Date

Data quality is very important for visualizations. Youll need to clean and preprocess your data to ensure its free from errors and anomalies. This process may include removing missing or duplicate values, data normalization, etc. Using uncleaned data could result in misinterpretation or incorrect conclusions  not to mention how difficult it is to create effective visualizations with it.

You wouldnt want to use dirty or outdated information to back decisions in your organization. Its also important to use the most recent and relevant data available to ensure your visualization is not only current, but accurate.

## What Are the Criteria for Good Data Visualizations?

Now that we know some best practices for creating data visualizations, here are some criteria for creating good data visualizations:

*   A good data visualization shows complex data connections in a way thats easy to understand, clear, concise and without clutter.
*   Your audience can quickly grasp the key points you are trying to communicate. Insights should be easily absorbed by your audience.
*   The visualizations should effectively communicate the information and ideas in the data using the right visual elements.
*   Good data visualizations should consider the needs of various audiences, while being accessible and inclusive by using clear and legible fonts and text sizes. Use appropriate color choices and contrasts. Avoid colors such as red and green, since red-green color blindness is most common.
*   A good data visualization is simple and straightforward without unnecessary distractions or elements.
*   Good data visualizations are based on accurate, current and reliable data.

## What Is the Best Data Visualization?

The best data visualization efficiently conveys the message youre trying to communicate. It considers the type of data involved and presents the data in a way thats easy to understand and interpret. It also considers design, readability and ease of comprehension.

## How to Judge a Good Data Visualization

Here are some criteria to consider when judging whether a data visualization is good:

*   Assess the visualizations use of color, labels and other design elements.
*   Are the texts readable and easy to understand, and do they provide adequate information?
*   Does it help your target audience understand the data and how to use it?
*   Are all the contents of the dashboard/visualization in accurate proportions?
*   Are the contents of the visualization legible for people with visual impairments?
*   Is the visualization easy to understand, uncluttered and engaging?
*   Do the colors in the visualization highlight key patterns?

## Conclusion

Data visualizations are key to observing and tracking metrics and KPIs in your organization. Following the best practices for putting together a data visualization will ensure you create reports that are easy to understand and helpful when pointing out patterns or anomalies. You can also check out this [post on best practices for dashboard design](https://www.influxdata.com/blog/5-dashboard-design-best-practices/?utm_source=vendor&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=2023-02_spnsr-ctn_7-best-practice-data-visualization_tns).
